***нажать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажа́ть</a> (2801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nažátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажимать.html>нажима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press, to push
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажми́те</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любой.html>любу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:клавиша.html>кла́вишу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nažmíte</b> ljubúju klávišu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Press</b> any key. (in computer games)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to urge, to impel, to influence, to put pressure on</li>
<li>to press on, to press ahead</li>
<li>to make by pressing</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажатый.html>нажа́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nažátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to reap, to harvest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nažátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нажина́ть</b>)

***нажимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нажимать.html>нажима́ть</a> (6087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажимать.html>нажима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nažimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press, to push</li>
<li>to urge, to impel, to influence, to put pressure on</li>
<li>to press on, to press ahead</li>
<li>to make by pressing</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.     <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сок.html>сок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фрукт.html>фруктов</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ягода.html>я́год</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п., приготавливать <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> каком-либо (</i><a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́м</a><i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:количество.html>коли́честве</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переходной.html>переходным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> непереходным <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажа́ть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нажраться.html>нажра́ться</a> (14560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нажра́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nažrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажраться.html>нажра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nažrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нажира́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat a lot, to eat one's fill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get very drunk</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нажра́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nažrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назвать.html>назва́вший</a> (601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назвать.html>назва́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazvávšij</span>)

***наземный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наземный.html>назе́мный</a> (12881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наземь.html>на́земь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">názemʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to the ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наземный.html>назе́мный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazémnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> land, ground, surface
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наземный.html>назе́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:транспорт.html>тра́нспорт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nazémnyj</b> tránsport</i> ― <span class="e-translation">surface transport, ground transportation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назначать.html>назнача́ть</a> (5024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naznáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначать.html>назнача́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naznačátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appoint, to designate, to nominate</li>
<li>to fix, to settle, to set, to assign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назначать.html>назнача́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naznačátʹ</b> srok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set a term, to set a deadline</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назначать.html>назнача́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naznačátʹ</b> pénsiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant a pension</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назначать.html>назнача́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naznačátʹ</b> posóbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant an allowance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to prescribe, to destine</li></ol>

***назначение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ние</a> (2430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naznáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naznačénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>appointment (act of appointing; designation of a person to hold an office)</li>
<li>fixing, setting, assignment</li>
<li>destination, purpose</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pharmacology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prescription</li></ol>

***назначить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a> (1679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naznáčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назначать.html>назнача́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appoint, to designate, to nominate</li>
<li>to fix, to settle, to set, to assign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naznáčitʹ</b> srok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set a term, to set a deadline</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naznáčitʹ</b> pénsiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant a pension</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назначить.html>назна́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naznáčitʹ</b> posóbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grant an allowance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to prescribe, to destine</li></ol>

***назойливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назойливый.html>назо́йливый</a> (9714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, original meaning may have been "noisy", in which case it may be derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зой</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scream</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зои́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rage, to rave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Both <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зой</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зои́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are ultimately related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зиять.html>зия́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zijátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to yawn, to gape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назойливый.html>назо́йливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazójlivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>irritating, intrusive, pushy</li></ol>

***назревать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a> (17208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazrevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen, to become ripe, to mature, (abscess) to come to a head</li>
<li>to be about to happen, to boil up, to be brewing</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-зре-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
